# Within the UNITY EDITOR:
# 1 - Drag and Drop the desired Image into the Unity Folder Assets/Resources/Images&Mats
# 2 - In the Assets/Resources/Images&Mats/Materials Folder, right click and hit Create > Material
# 3 - Rename that material to the name of the desired image (this name should be identical to the one found in the DBVI text file)
# 4 - Click on the Material to have its properties appear in the Inspector on the left hand side, and change the Rendering Mode from Opaque to Cutout
# 5 - Click on the small gear to the left of the Albedo property to open the 'Select Texture' explorer window, and select the image you initially dragged into Assets/Resources/Images&Mats
# 6 - Ensure that the Albedo itself is Black (RGB 0, 0, 0) to better define the original color of the desired image. Adjustable until you feel the image is clearest once in-game
